											add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = migration_attraction97_75}
										}
										else = { 
											if = { limit = {migration_attraction<98.25 }
												add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = migration_attraction98_0}
											}
											else = { 
												add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = migration_attraction98_25}
											}
										}
									}
								}
								else = { 
									if = { limit = {migration_attraction<99.25 }
										if = { limit = {migration_attraction<98.75 }
											add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = migration_attraction98_5}
										}
										else = { 
											if = { limit = {migration_attraction<99.0 }
												add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = migration_attraction98_75}
											}
											else = { 
												add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = migration_attraction99_0}
											}
										}
									}
									else = { 
										if = { limit = {migration_attraction<99.75 }
											if = { limit = {migration_attraction<99.5 }
												add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = migration_attraction99_25}
											}
											else = { 
												add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = migration_attraction99_5}
											}
										}
										else = { 
											if = { limit = {migration_attraction<100.0 }
												add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = migration_attraction99_75}
											}
											else = { 
												add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = migration_attraction100_0}
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
    }
}
        
update_pop_growth.2 = {
	type = country_event
	hidden = yes
    
    trigger = {tag = ROM}
	
	immediate = { 
        every_province = {
            trigger_event = { id = update_pop_growth.1 }
        }
    }
}
